These objects may be filled with solid colors, patterns, radial or linear color gradients and their borders may be stroked, both with adjustable transparency. Embedding and optional tracing of raster graphics is also supported, enabling the editor to create vector graphics from photos and other raster sources. Created shapes can be further manipulated with transformations, such as moving, rotating, scaling and skewing.\r\n\r\nhttps://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Inkscape\r\n\r\nYou can support Inkscape! https://inkscape.org/en/support-us/donate/","ProductFamilyName":"Apps","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9WZDNCRFHX52","TileLayout":"Square","Title":"Network Speed Test","Images":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.13863.9007199266247335.56f360b7-b4ea-40cb-a5e7-aad3a9b4d929.5011315f-6bfb-45e4-83ff-36aa145ffa8b","Height":150,"Width":150,"BackgroundColor":"#009E49","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.58124.9007199266247335.34c156b4-4f1a-42fc-8f64-c889b37f5926.8e9f665b-984f-4cdc-83c4-7cc24ce84804","Height":150,"Width":310,"BackgroundColor":"#009E49","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""}],"DisplayPrice":"Free","Price":0.0,"AverageRating":0.0,"RatingsCount":"0","PackageFamilyNames":["Microsoft.NetworkSpeedTest_8wekyb3d8bbwe"],"ContentIds":["6f22b67c-228d-89de-29a5-5ab1fbec5718"],"GamingOptionsXboxLive":false,"AvailableDevicesDisplayText":"","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"PC","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"How fast is your Internet connection?\r\n\r\nNetwork Speed Test measures your network delay, download speed and upload speed.\r\n\r\nUsing servers all over the world, Network Speed Test measures your network connection’s latency and throughput.
